add_namespace = ww1_qing
add_namespace = qing_news

#KMT Rice Easter Egg
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.433.t
	desc = ww1_qing.433.d
	
	id = ww1_qing.433

	picture = GFX_report_event_kmt_rice
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_fractured
			days > 720
		}
		NOT = {
			has_active_mission = QIN_xinhai_timer
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.433.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}
#Chen Kuilong
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.432.t
	desc = ww1_qing.432.d
	
	id = ww1_qing.432

	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.432.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = 0.01
		if = {
			limit = {
				QIN = { has_idea = QIN_idea_improved_trade }
			}
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = QIN_idea_improved_trade
				days = 80
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = QIN_idea_improved_trade
				days = 80
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.432.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_stability = -0.03
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_zhang_zhenfang
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.432.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_political_power = 50
		
	}
}
#Send Duanfang South
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.431.t
	desc = ww1_qing.431.d
	
	id = ww1_qing.431

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.431.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 150 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		QIN_xinhai_timer_-25 = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_move_hubei
		hidden_effect = {
			QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.183 days = 8 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.178.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0 
		}
		QIN_xinhai_timer_-25 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.181 days = 10 } }
				}
				35 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						has_completed_focus = QIN_local_government_reform
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_legality
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_fair_punishment
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_unfair_punishment
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_guangzhou_democratic_accept
					}
					QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.182 days = 10 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.178.c
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}
#Hankou Conference
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.430.t
	desc = ww1_qing.430.d
	id = ww1_qing.430

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
		has_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
		}
		
		fascism > 0.75
		
		has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_2 }
	}
	immediate = {
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 50
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_2
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.430.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.430.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.2
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai
		#custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_cancel_invite_shikai
		clr_global_flag = QIN_autocomplete_appoint_shikai
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = QIN_yuan_shikai
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			QIN_yuan_shikai = {
				add_unit_leader_trait = sick
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
			
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.291 hours = 3 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3
		} 
		custom_effect_tooltip = line_description
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.425 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us4
		CHI = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us2
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us3
	}
}
#Royalist Protest
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.429.t
	desc = ww1_qing.429.d
	id = ww1_qing.429

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
		has_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
		}
		
		fascism > 0.75
		
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_1 }
	}
	immediate = {
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 50
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_1
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.429.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.005
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_court_would_oppose_this_but_no
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.429.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_war_support = -0.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_court_would_oppose_this_but_no
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.429.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.15
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai
		#custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_cancel_invite_shikai
		clr_global_flag = QIN_autocomplete_appoint_shikai
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = QIN_yuan_shikai
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			QIN_yuan_shikai = {
				add_unit_leader_trait = sick
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
			
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.291 hours = 3 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3
		} 
		custom_effect_tooltip = line_description
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.425 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us4
		CHI = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us2
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us3
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		is_qing_monarchy = yes
		date > 1912.2.3
		608 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = QIN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
		}
		#NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_reform_the_civil_service_exam }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.428.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.432
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

#Shandong Surrenders
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.427.t
	desc = ww1_qing.427.d
	
	id = ww1_qing.427

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		597 = {
			is_owned_by = CHI
			is_controlled_by = QIN
		}
		has_war_with = CHI
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			transfer_state = 597
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.427.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		CHI = {
			add_war_support = -0.1
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "Shandong Provincial Army"
			division_names_group = CHI_GAR_02
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			support = {
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			}
		}
		597 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Shandong New Army\" division_template = \"Shandong Provincial Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
				owner = QIN
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Jinan New Army\" division_template = \"Shandong Provincial Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
				owner = QIN
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.427.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		QIN_shandong_rebel_improve = yes
				division_template = {
			name = "Shandong Provincial Army"
			division_names_group = CHI_GAR_02
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			support = {
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			}
		}
		597 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Shandong New Army\" division_template = \"Shandong Provincial Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
				owner = QIN
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Jinan New Army\" division_template = \"Shandong Provincial Army\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
				owner = QIN
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.427.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		QIN_shandong_rebel_improve = yes
		QIN_shandong_rebel_improve = yes
	}
}
#Triple Revolt
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.426.t
	desc = ww1_qing.426.d
	id = ww1_qing.426
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = triple_revolution
		}
		has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		date > 1913.5.30
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_hui_during_xinhai
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.426.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_triple_revolt_now
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.101 #Hui Merchants
				days = 15
				random_days = 30
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.109 #Ma Support
				days = 15
				random_days = 30
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.105 #Triple Revolt
				days = 60
				random_days = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.426.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_hui_during_xinhai
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_triple_revolt_delay
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = QIN_idea_diverted_garrisons
			days = 200
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.426.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_hui_during_xinhai
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_triple_revolt_delay_bonus
		add_stability = -0.025
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_triple_revolt_delay
	}
}
#Beiyang Deal - CHINA
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.425.t
	desc = ww1_qing.425.d
	id = ww1_qing.425
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.425.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us22
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			CHI_yuan_shikai = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIN = {
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
					disband = no
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Xinjian Lujun (Beiyang Army)"
					disband = no
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
					}
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				QIN_yuan_shikai = {
					retire = yes
				}
				QIN_zhao_bingjun = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				QIN_wang_shizhen = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
			CHI = {
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Xinjian Lujun (Beiyang Army)"
					disband = yes
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Xinjian Lujun (Beiyang Army)"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					template_counter = 0
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Xinjian Lujun (Beiyang Army)\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no
						count = 25
					}
					
				}
				CHI_yuan_shikai = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = oligarchism
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_fascism_party
					name = CHI_fascism_party
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.425.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#Cheong Fatt Tze's Investment
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.424.t
	desc = ww1_qing.424.d
	id = ww1_qing.424
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.424.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_cheong_investment
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Cheong Fatt Tze in Hong Kong
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.422.t
	desc = ww1_qing.422.d
	id = ww1_qing.422
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 80
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_election_generic
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		date > 1915.1.5
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_cheong_dead
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.422.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

#Xinhai from too much Democratic Support!!!
country_event = {
	id = ww1_qing.416
	hidden = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		
		has_global_flag = QIN_flag_democratic_disaster
		NOT = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_agreement
			has_completed_focus = QIN_crush_the_tongmenghui
		}
		
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = {
				flag = xinhai_revolution
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				democratic > 0.71
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_agreement
					has_completed_focus = QIN_crush_the_tongmenghui
				}
				
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = {
						flag = xinhai_revolution
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai }
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = CHI_rebellion_province
					min = 1
					max = 6
					integer = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_xinhai.2
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_revolution_location
		}
		else = {
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_democratic_disaster
	}
}

		tag = QIN

		NOT = {
			has_variable = var_henan_rebel
			has_variable = var_hunan_rebel
			has_variable = var_jiangsu_rebel
			has_variable = var_guangxi_rebel
			has_variable = var_sichuan_rebel
			has_variable = var_yunnan_rebel
			has_variable = var_zhejiang_rebel
			has_variable = var_shaanxi_rebel
			has_variable = var_shandong_rebel
		}
		
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			play_song = "beiyang_fleet_anthem"
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_provincial_unity
	}

		add_stability = 0.15

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.176.t
	desc = ww1_qing.176.d
	id = ww1_qing.176
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_army_training
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.375
				days = 10
				random_days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = QIN
		date < 1911.8.10
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = guangzhou_uprising
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.176.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_stability = -0.1
		QIN_xinhai_timer_30 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_announce_reform }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_announce_reform
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.176.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_guangzhou_democratic_accept
		add_stability = -0.05		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.125
		}
		add_political_power = -75
	}
}

	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.371.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_efficient_government }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.371.d
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = QIN_efficient_government
		}
	}
	
	id = ww1_qing.371

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.371.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_efficient_government }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_government_trials }
			}
			complete_national_focus = QIN_government_trials
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_crackdown_on_bribery }
			}
			complete_national_focus = QIN_crackdown_on_bribery
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_appointment_by_merit }
			}
			complete_national_focus = QIN_appointment_by_merit
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.12
		}
		set_global_flag = chen_chunxuan_sichuan_governor
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.371.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.005
		QIN_sichuan_rebel_down = yes
	}
}

# Anti-Sun Faction - Tongmenghui Fracture
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.359.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.359.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIN_assasinate_sun_yat_sen }
		}
	}	
	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.359.d2
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = QIN_assasinate_sun_yat_sen
		}
	}	
	id = ww1_qing.359

	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_tongmenghui
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_fractured
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		OR = {
			OR = {
				date > 1915.1.1
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
						has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
						has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
						has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
						has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
					}
					democratic < 0.2
				}
				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_xinhai_just_ended
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_agreement }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.359.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = QIN_diminish_the_kuomintang 
				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_chose_devitalize
			QIN_xinhai_timer_200 = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
					add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
					add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
					add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
					add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
				}
				remove_ideas = { QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_completed_focus = QIN_diminish_the_kuomintang 
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_chose_devitalize
			QIN_xinhai_timer_150 = yes
		}
		else = {
			QIN_xinhai_timer_100 = yes
		}
	}
}

# Yuan Shikai's Cabinet
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.352.t
	desc = ww1_qing.352.d
	id = ww1_qing.352
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.352.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury
				add_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2
				add_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3
		} 
		
		QIN_yuan_shikai = {
			add_trait = {
				trait = QIN_beiyang_cabinet
			}
		}
		#custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_beiyang_last_chance
		set_global_flag = QIN_beiyang_last_chance
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.350.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai
		#custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_cancel_invite_shikai
		clr_global_flag = QIN_autocomplete_appoint_shikai
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = QIN_yuan_shikai
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			QIN_yuan_shikai = {
				add_unit_leader_trait = sick
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
			
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.291 hours = 3 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_2

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_yuan_shikai_foot_injury_3
		} 
		custom_effect_tooltip = line_description
		CHI = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.425 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_yuan_shikai_will_betray_us4
		CHI = {

#China Unequal Treaties
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.347.t
	desc = ww1_qing.347.d
	id = ww1_qing.347
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_qing_boxer_rebellion
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends
				CHI = {
					has_country_flag = xinhai_victory
				}
			}
			QIN = { has_completed_focus = QIN_coup_the_government }
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_1914_situation }
		OR = {
			QIN = {
				has_country_flag = qing_russian_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_german_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_french_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_british_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_japanese_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_american_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_italian_concession
				has_country_flag = qing_austrian_concession
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = unequal_treaties_dm }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_consumer_goods = 0.38 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_research_speed = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_resources_to_market = 0.88 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_infrastructure = -0.12 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_military_factory = -0.25 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_civilian_factory = -0.25 }
			set_variable = { unequal_treaties_dockyard = -0.25 }
			set_country_flag = qing_russian_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_german_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_french_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_british_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_japanese_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_american_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_italian_concession
			set_country_flag = qing_austrian_concession
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_russian_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_russian_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_german_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_german_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_british_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_british_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_french_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_french_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_italian_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_italian_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_japanese_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_japanese_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_american_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_american_concession = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_austrian_concession } }
				}
				QIN_end_austrian_concession = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.347.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_ideas = unequal_treaties
	}
}

			}
		}
		891 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.311.t
	desc = ww1_qing.311.d
	id = ww1_qing.311
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		QIN = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.311.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_italian
		}
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_usa
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_french
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 591
						state = 594
						state = 728
					}
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
				transfer_state_to = FRA
			}
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_british
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 326
						state = 592
						state = 746
					}
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
				transfer_state_to = ENG
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_german
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 872
						state = 745
					}
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
				transfer_state_to = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }

			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 329
						state = 330
					}
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
				transfer_state_to = RUS
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner } }
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_payments_of_indemnities_japan
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 745
						state = 872
						state = 716
						state = 744
						state = 524
					}
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
				transfer_state_to = JAP
			}
		}
	}

#New Regent
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.291.t
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.291.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = QIN_zaifeng
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_qing.291.d
	}
	id = ww1_qing.291
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_qing_zaifeng
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = QIN_xuantong
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = QIN_zaifeng
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
					has_stability < 0.05
					has_political_power < -275
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
			}
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_court_yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_selecting_regent
		#clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.291.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_selecting_regent
		trigger = {
			has_character = QIN_longyu
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { can_be_country_leader = QIN_longyu }
			}
			QIN_longyu = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = autocracy
						traits = {
							court_conservative
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = QIN_longyu
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = QIN_expand_parliament
						has_completed_focus = QIN_empower_the_empire_unity_party
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.291.c
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_selecting_regent
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			has_character = QIN_yikuang
		}
		promote_character = QIN_yikuang
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = QIN_expand_parliament
						has_completed_focus = QIN_empower_the_empire_unity_party
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.291.b
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_need_new_regent
		clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_selecting_regent
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { can_be_country_leader = QIN_natong }
			}
			QIN_natong = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = autocracy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = QIN_natong
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = QIN_expand_parliament
						has_completed_focus = QIN_empower_the_empire_unity_party
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = ww1_qing.248.d
	id = ww1_qing.248
	
	timeout_days = 100
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_national_academy_of_sciences
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.248.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50 
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_fair_punishment
		add_to_variable = {
			var = QIN_var_legal_reform
			value = 1
			tooltip = QIN_effect_var_legal_reform_up
		}
		QIN_court_opp_50 = yes
		
		#variable check
		add_to_variable = {
			var = QIN_var_legal_reform_completed
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { QIN_var_legal_reform_completed = 5 }
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_judicial_reform_completed
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.248.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 150 
		}
		
		QIN_lower_opp_50 = yes
		
		#variable check
		add_to_variable = {
			var = QIN_var_legal_reform_completed
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { QIN_var_legal_reform_completed = 5 }
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_judicial_reform_completed
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.248.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = QIN_var_legal_reform
			value = -1
			tooltip = QIN_effect_var_legal_reform_down
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
					add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
			}
			remove_ideas =  QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
		}
		QIN_lower_opp_75 = yes
		
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_unfair_punishment
		#variable check
		add_to_variable = {
			var = QIN_var_legal_reform_completed
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { QIN_var_legal_reform_completed = 5 }
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_judicial_reform_completed
		}
	}
}

		days = 25
	}

		original_tag = QIN
		QIN_yuan_shikai = {
			OR = {
				is_leading_army = yes
				is_leading_army_group = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_shikai_invite }
	}

		name = ww1_qing.225.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_qing.220
	title = ww1_china.123.t
	desc = ww1_china.123.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# social democratic
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.123.a
		trigger = {
			has_character = QIN_sun_yatsen
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
				has_country_flag = sun_yatsen_president
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
					name = CHI_kuomintang_party
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		QIN_sun_yatsen = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					ideology = socialism
					traits = { father_of_the_republic }
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_president
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.123.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.219.t
	desc = ww1_qing.219.d
	id = ww1_qing.219
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.219.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		QIN_xinhai_timer_30 = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_owned_state = { is_on_continent = europe }
					tag = USA
					tag = CAN
					tag = AST
				}
				NOT = { tag = TUR }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = QIN
				modifier = QIN_opinion_protect_christian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = ww1_qing.219.b
		add_stability = 0.07
		add_war_support = 0.07
		QIN_xinhai_timer_-100 = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_owned_state = { is_on_continent = europe }
					tag = USA
					tag = CAN
					tag = AST
				}
				NOT = { tag = TUR }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = QIN
				modifier = QIN_opinion_christian_no
			}
		}
		
	}
}
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.218.t
	desc = ww1_qing.218.d
	id = ww1_qing.218
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = ww1_qing.218.a
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_agreement
		QIN_xinhai_timer_300 = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5 }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
		}
		add_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_agreement
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.215.t
	desc = ww1_qing.215.d
	id = ww1_qing.215
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	picture = QIN_qing_court_members_image
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		CHI = { exists = no }
		QIN = { has_country_flag = xinhai_victory }
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_xinhai_just_ended
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai } 
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_already_played_pu_tian_yue
					}
				}
			

				play_song = "pu_tian_yue"
				set_global_flag = QIN_flag_already_played_pu_tian_yue
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_qing.405 
					days = 20
					random_days = 15
					random_hours = 5
				}	
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = ww1_qing.359 
				days = 5
				random_days = 5
				random_hours = 24
			}	
			
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.215.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }	
		add_political_power = 150
		add_war_support = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_disloyalty
				}
				clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
				clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_disloyalty
				delete_units = {
					division_template = "Xinjian Lujun (Beiyang Army)"
					disband = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_qing_monarchy = yes
					has_country_leader = {
						character = QIN_yuan_shikai
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					NOT = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_qing.417
					days = 2
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_reorganize
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_don't_trigger_xinhai_again
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_failed_to_take_nanjing
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_defection
			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tongmenghui_split
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai 
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai 
				}
				clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_accept_shikai
			}
			clr_global_flag = QIN_third_uprising
			clr_global_flag = QIN_next_uprising
			clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_court_panic
			
			annex_country = {
				target = TIB
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = QIN_third_option
				}
			}
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Feng Guozhang Army"
			disband = no
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Loyalist Militia"
			disband = no
		}
		
		clr_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		clr_global_flag = QIN_chosen
		clr_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends
		set_global_flag = QIN_warlord_watch
		clear_variable = CHI_xinhai_name_solid
		
		CHI = {
			clr_country_flag = second_uprising
			clr_country_flag = third_uprising
		}
		QIN = {
			clr_country_flag = second_uprising
			clr_country_flag = third_uprising
		}
		QIN = { clr_country_flag = xinhai_victory }
		complete_national_focus = QIN_restore_the_nation

# Death of Yiquang
country_event = {
	id = ww1_qing.209
	title = ww1_qing.209.t
	desc = ww1_qing.209.d
	picture = QIN_report_event_qing_funeral
	trigger = {
		is_china_or_warlord = yes
		OR = {
			is_qing_monarchy = yes
			has_idea = QIN_abdicated_qing_imperial_family
			has_idea = QIN_abdicated_qing_imperial_family2
		}
		date > 1917.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = yiquang_death }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 28
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.209.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = QIN
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = QIN_zhang_xun
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = QIN_xuantong
						}
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = QIN_yikuang
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = QIN_appoint_kang_youwei
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = QIN_kang_youwei
						}
						QIN_kang_youwei = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_ideology = autocracy
								}
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = autocracy
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								promote_character = autocracy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				# placeholder, since yiquang dies before xuantong become adult
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = QIN_natong
					}
					QIN_natong = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = autocracy
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = QIN_yikuang
				}
				retire_character = QIN_yikuang
			}
			set_global_flag = yiquang_death
		}
	}
}

	}

			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_waited_3
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_waited_2

		}

				has_global_flag = QIN_flag_waited_1

			set_global_flag = QIN_flag_waited_2

		QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.264 days = 180 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_delay_decision
	}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.191.t
	desc = ww1_qing.191.d
	id = ww1_qing.191
	 
	timeout_days = 100
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#picture = 
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.191.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 35 
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		QIN_xinhai_timer_25 = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.191.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0 
		}
		add_stability = 0.025
		QIN_xinhai_timer_25 = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = THIS
				modifier = QIN_opinion_encourage_travel
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = QIN_opinion_encourage_travel
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.191.c
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0 
		}
		add_stability = -0.075
		QIN_xinhai_timer_75 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
			has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
			has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
			has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
			has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
				add_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
			has_idea = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
			}
			remove_ideas = { QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5 }
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = THIS
				modifier = QIN_opinion_ban_travel
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = QIN_opinion_ban_travel
		}
	}
}

# Disaster in Hubei!
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.183.t
	desc = ww1_qing.183.d
	id = ww1_qing.183
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = zhao_erfeng_dead
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.420
				days = 7
				random_days = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
				}
				set_global_flag = wuchang_uprising
				603 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				607 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				600 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.183.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 15 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = QIN_idea_announce_reform }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_announce_reform
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line_description
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_wuchang_descr
		activate_mission_tooltip = QIN_wuchang_timer
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 325
						state = 593
						state = 605
						state = 620
					}
				}
				set_border_war = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.183.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

# Railway Protection Movement
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.177.t
	desc = ww1_qing.177.desc
	id = ww1_qing.177
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_infiltration
	trigger = {
		original_tag = QIN
		date > 1911.8.11
		NOT = { QIN = { has_completed_focus = QIN_leave_railways_to_the_provinces } }
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = guangzhou_uprising
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.177.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = zhao_erfeng_governor_of_sichuan
				}
				random_list = {
					88 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.178 days = 10 } }
					}
					5 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 3.0
							NOT = { has_variable = QIN_var_sichuan_rebel }
						}

							factor = 2.0
							has_army_size = {
								size > 45
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2.0
							has_completed_focus = QIN_local_government_reform
						}
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.179 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = zhao_erxun_governor_of_sichuan
				}
				random_list = {
					88 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.178 days = 10 } }
					}
					15 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 2.0
							has_completed_focus = QIN_local_government_reform
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2.0
							has_global_flag = QIN_flag_legality
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2.0
							has_global_flag = QIN_flag_fair_punishment
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.5
							has_global_flag = QIN_flag_unfair_punishment
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2.0
							has_global_flag = QIN_flag_guangzhou_democratic_accept
						}
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.179 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					605 = {
						infrastructure > 4
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					88 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.178 days = 10 } }
					}
					17 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.179 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					88 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.178 days = 10 } }
					}
					10 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.179 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.177.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}
		QIN_xinhai_timer_-50 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = QIN_nationalize_railways }
			remove_ideas = QIN_idea_railway_profits
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		
			if = {
				limit = {
					605 = {
						infrastructure > 4
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					45 = {

					}
					17 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.180 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.178 days = 10 } }
					}
					15 = {
						QIN = { country_event = { id = ww1_qing.180 days = 10 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.177.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = QIN_nationalize_railways }

		add_political_power = -10
	}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.155.t
	desc = ww1_qing.155.d
	id = ww1_qing.155

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.155.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		QIN_xinhai_timer_25 = yes
	}
}
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.154.t
	desc = ww1_qing.154.d
	id = ww1_qing.154

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.154.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = JAP
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		QIN_xinhai_timer_200 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = korea_fight
			}
			
			JAP = {
			end_puppet = KOR
			KOR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				add_to_faction = KOR
			}
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.60 days = 0 }
			}
		}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.154.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.153.t
	desc = ww1_qing.153.d
	id = ww1_qing.153

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.153.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		QIN = {
			JAP = {
				release = KOR
				QIN = {
					puppet = KOR
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.155 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.153.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
				naval_strength_ratio = {
				tag = JAP
				ratio > 1
				}
				JAP = {
					is_subject_of = QIN
				}
				}
			}
		}
		QIN = {
		country_event = { id = ww1_qing.154 days = 0 }
		}
	}
}

#Italian Indemnities
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.146.t
	desc = ww1_qing.146.d
	id = ww1_qing.146
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_italian_concession }
		ITA = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = QIN
				is_subject_of = QIN
				has_civil_war = yes
				exists = no
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.146.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		QIN_end_italian_concession = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.140.t
	desc = ww1_qing.146.d
	id = ww1_qing.140

	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		QIN = { has_country_flag = qing_german_concession }
		GER = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = QIN
				is_subject_of = QIN
				has_civil_war = yes
				exists = no
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

#Triple Revolution
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.105.t
	desc = ww1_qing.105.d
	id = ww1_qing.105
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_battle
	
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		date < 1916.1.1
		is_subject = no
		
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = minority_rebellion_prevented
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.383
				days = 3
				random_days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.102
				days = 10
				random_days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.107
				days = 11
				random_days = 25
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_qing.106
				days = 6
				random_days = 5
			}
	
		
			set_global_flag = triple_revolution
			if = {
				limit = {
					TIB = {
						exists = no
					}
					322 = {
						is_owned_by = QIN
					}
				}
				QIN = {
					release = TIB
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				release = SIK
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					SIK = { is_subject_of = QIN } 
				}
				end_puppet = SIK
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
				
					TIB = { 
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = QIN 
					} 
				}
				end_puppet = TIB
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = mongolia_integrated
					}
					330 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = QIN }
				}

						set_province_controller = 1855
						set_province_controller = 7808
						set_province_controller = 7870

						set_province_controller = 12520
						set_province_controller = 7843
						set_province_controller = 12695
						set_province_controller = 7773
						set_province_controller = 1877
						set_province_controller = 1689
						set_province_controller = 12520
						set_province_controller = 10669
						set_province_controller = 4777
						set_province_controller = 10563
						set_province_controller = 10695
						set_province_controller = 4751
						set_province_controller = 10539
						set_province_controller = 12544
						set_province_controller = 7799
						load_oob = QIN_triple_revolt_mon
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = mongolia_integrated
					}
					MON = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = QIN
					}
				}
				end_puppet = MON
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						329 = {
							owner = { is_subject_of = QIN }
						}
						329 = {
							owner = { tag = QIN }
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = mongolia_integrated
					}
				}
				MON = {
					transfer_state = 329
				}
			}
			SIK = {
				set_capital = { state = 287 }
				inherit_technology = QIN
				set_research_slots = 2
				set_cosmetic_tag = QIN_hui_revolt
				hidden_effect = {
					load_oob = "TIB_army"
					load_oob = "QIN_triple_revolt"
					#load_oob = "QIN_triple_revolt"
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment_0
						amount = 1850
						producer = CHI
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 300
						producer = CHI
					}
				}
				
			}
			SIK = {
				create_faction = "Triple Revolt"
				if = {
					limit = {
						MON = {
							is_subject = no
							is_in_faction = no
						}
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = mongolia_integrated
						}
					}
					add_to_faction = MON
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TIB = {
							is_subject = no
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}

				}
				SIK = { transfer_state = 755 }
				SIK = { transfer_state = 894 }
				
				declare_war_on = {
					target = QIN
					type = annex_everything
				}	
				287 = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = QIN
						}
						to_state = 621
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = mongolia_integrated
					}
					MON = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = SIK
					}
				}
				MON = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = QIN
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					TIB = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = SIK
					}
				}
				TIB = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = QIN
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			TIB = {
				hidden_effect = {
					load_oob = "TIB_army"
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment_0
						amount = 500
						producer = CHI
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CHI = { exists = yes }
					NOT = { TIB = { is_guaranteed_by = ENG } }
				}
				CHI = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SIK
						type = annex_everything
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TIB
						type = annex_everything
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = MON
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.105.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}

# Japan refuses split
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.96.t
	desc = ww1_qing.96.d
	id = ww1_qing.96
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.96.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.96.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { QIN = { is_subject_of = JAP } }
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
		  focus = QIN_sino_japanese_friendship_act
		  uncomplete_children = yes
		  refund_political_power = no
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tried_friendship
		if = {
			limit = {
				QIN = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction= yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					num_faction_members < 3
				}
			}
			JAP = { dismantle_faction = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					527 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = JAP
					}
					KOR = {
						527 = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = KOR
						}
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				transfer_state = 527
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
				799 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = JAP
				}
				KOR = {
				AND = {
				799 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = KOR
				}
				is_subject_of = JAP
				}
				}
				}
			}
			QIN = {
			transfer_state = 799
			}			
		}
			
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.95.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		QIN = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.96 days = 0 }	
		}
		
	}
}

# Japan refuses to return taiwan - Peaceful path
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.92.t
	desc = ww1_qing.92.d
	id = ww1_qing.92
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.93.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.93.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { QIN = { is_subject_of = JAP } }
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
		  focus = QIN_sino_japanese_friendship_act
		  uncomplete_children = yes
		  refund_political_power = no
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tried_friendship
		if = {
			limit = {
				QIN = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction= yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					num_faction_members < 3
				}
			}
			JAP = { dismantle_faction = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

			create_faction = "East-Asia Pact"
			add_to_faction = QIN
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = QIN_idea_new_alliance
				days = 500
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = QIN_idea_trust_concern
				days = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.86.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { QIN = { is_subject_of = JAP } }
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.87 days = 0 }
		}
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
		  focus = QIN_sino_japanese_friendship_act
		  uncomplete_children = yes
		  refund_political_power = no
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_tried_friendship
		if = {
			limit = {
				QIN = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction= yes
		}
		if = {

				JAP = {
					is_faction_leader = yes

country_event = { #Qing offers Siam alliance for land
	title = ww1_qing.66.t
	desc = ww1_qing.66.d
	id = ww1_qing.66

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.66.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				QIN = {
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 822	
						controls_state = 670
						controls_state = 819
						controls_state = 820
						controls_state = 843
						controls_state = 640
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 822	
					state = 670
					state = 819
					state = 820
					state = 843
					state = 640
					state = 741
				}
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = QIN
			}
			set_state_owner_to = SIA
			add_core_of = SIA
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = { is_controlled_by = QIN }
				}
					
				set_state_controller_to = SIA
			}
		}
		QIN = { puppet = SIA }
		set_autonomy = {
			target = SIA
			autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_associate 
			end_wars = no
			end_civil_wars = no
		}
		QIN = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.68 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.66.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 3 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				QIN = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = SIA
						ratio > 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		QIN = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.67 days = 0 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_qing.257
	hidden = yes
	title = ww1_korea.20.t
	desc = ww1_korea.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_parade
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_korea.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = KOR
			KOR = { leave_faction = yes }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KOR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			QIN = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 5
					name = ww1_korea.20.t
				}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 799 }
			white_peace = QIN
		}
		KOR = {
			give_military_access = QIN
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0
			states = {
				525
				796
				797
				800
				801
				802
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = JAP_samurai_lineage
				}
			}
			keep_political_party_members = yes
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = KOR
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_country_flag = civil_war_japanese_korea
		}
		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = KOR_provisional_government_long
			name = KOR_provisional_government
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = KOR_fascism_party_long
			name = KOR_fascism_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascism
			long_name = KOR_fascism_party_long
			name = KOR_fascism_party
		}
		KOR_hong_beomdo = {
			promote_character = stratocracy
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}	
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.7
		}
		set_war_support = 0.8
		set_stability = 0.9
		division_template = {
			name = "Dongnipgun"
			regiments = {
				infantry = {
					x = 0
					y = 0
				}
				infantry = {
					x = 1
					y = 0
				}
				infantry = {
					x = 0
					y = 1
				}
				infantry = {
					x = 1
					y = 1
				}
			}
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "Uibyeong"
			regiments = {
				militia = {
					x = 0
					y = 0
				}
				militia = {
					x = 0
					y = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_division_template_lock = {
			division_template = "Dongnipgun"
			is_locked = no
		}
		set_division_template_lock = {
			division_template = "Uibyeong"
			is_locked = yes
		}
		799 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"1. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"2. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"3. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
		}
		527 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"4. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"5. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"6. Dongnipgun\" division_template = \"Dongnipgun\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				owner = KOR
			}
		}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.262.t
	desc = ww1_qing.262.d
	id = ww1_qing.262
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_japanese_handshake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.262.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				is_core_of = QIN
			}
			transfer_state_to = QIN
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = { 
					exists = yes 
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KOR
					owner = {
						has_war_with = QIN
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = KOR
			}
			KOR = { set_capital = { state = 800 } }
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KOR
					owner = {
						has_war_with = QIN
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = QIN
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				409 = {
					is_owned_by = QIN
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					655 = {
						is_owned_by = JAP
					}
				}
				655 = { transfer_state_to = QIN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					537 = {
						is_owned_by = JAP
					}
				}
				537 = { transfer_state_to = QIN }
			}
		}
		QIN = { white_peace = JAP }
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
			KOR = { white_peace = JAP }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_royals_in_japan }
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.276 days = 0 }	
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.262.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		JAP = { add_war_support = 0.15 }
	}
}

#Second Sino-Japanese war peace
country_event = {
	title = ww1_qing.259.t
	desc = ww1_qing.259.d
	id = ww1_qing.259
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		OR = {
			AND = {
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = KOR }
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = QIN
								has_war_with = JAP
							}
						}
						controller = {
							has_war_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				any_state = {
					is_core_of = KOR
					owner = {
						has_war_with = QIN
					}
				}
			}
			524 = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				is_fully_controlled_by = QIN
			}
			any_state = {
				is_owned_by = JAP
				region = 154
				is_controlled_by = QIN
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = QIN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.259.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		QIN = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_qing.262 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.259.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				country_event = { id = ww1_qing.260 days = 0 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			QIN = {
				country_event = { id = ww1_qing.261 days = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_parade

	fire_only_once = yes	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.2.a
		remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = QIN_idea_purge days = 720 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.2.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
			add_idea = QIN_idea_beiyang_army_2
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 744 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 744 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 745 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 745 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 326 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 326 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 729 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 729 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 728 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 728 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 524 }
			QIN = { transfer_state = 524 }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_qing.4.b
		QIN = { country_event = ww1_qing.5 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				QIN = { has_army_manpower = { size < 750000 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				original_tag = OST
			}
		}
	}
}
